                      function actShowBookDetail(value, obj) {\n                            var css = {\n                                'position': 'absolute',\n                                'z-index': '1',\n                                'top': '52px',\n                                'left': (value == 0) ? '82px' : '48px'\n                            };\n                            $('ul.book-box', obj).css(css).slideDown('slow', function () {\n                                $(this).removeClass('hide');\n                            });\n                        }\n\n                        $('a.attend').live('click', function (e) {\n                            e.preventDefault();\n                            var thisObj = $(this);\n                            var curActObj = thisObj.closest('.activityitem');\n                            var prObj = thisObj.closest('.activityitem').find('.book-box');\n                            thisObj.closest('.activityitem').addClass('current');\n                            if ($(this).hasClass('clicked')) {\n                                if (confirm('แน่ใจจิง ๆ นะ !!')) {\n                                    $('ul.book-box').slideUp('slow', function () {\n                                        $(this).addClass('hide');\n                                    });\n                                    var param = {mode: 'cancel', id: $('#a_id', prObj).val()};\n                                    $.ajax({\n                                        type: \"POST\",\n                                        url: \"/ajax/updateBookmark.php\",\n                                        data: param,\n                                        dataType: 'json',\n                                        success: function (res) {\n                                            if (res.status == false) {\n                                                alert(res.msg);\n                                                return;\n                                            } else {\n                                                thisObj.removeClass('clicked');\n                                                //$('.dil_lll, .tempword', curActObj).remove();\n                                                curActObj.find('.textdetailbig').eq(0).html(res.contents);\n                                            }\n                                        }\n                                    });\n                                }\n                            } else {\n                                actShowBookDetail(Number($(this).attr('val')), curActObj);\n                            }\n                        });\n\n                        $('ul.book-box a.submit').live('click', function (e) {\n                            e.preventDefault();\n                            var prObj = $(this).closest('.book-box');\n                            var curActObj = prObj.closest('.current');\n                            var event_type = (Math.ceil(prObj.position().left) == 82) ? 0 : 1;\n                            var mode = 'insert';\n                            if ($('a.attend.clicked', curActObj).length > 0) {\n                                mode = 'edit';\n                            }\n                            var param = {mode: mode, id: $('#a_id', prObj).val(), show: $('#startshow', prObj).val(), alerttime: $('#date_alert', prObj).val(), event_type: event_type};\n                            $.ajax({\n                                type: \"POST\",\n                                url: \"/ajax/updateBookmark.php\",\n                                data: param,\n                                dataType: 'json',\n                                success: function (res) {\n                                    if (res.status == false) {\n                                        alert(res.msg);\n                                        return;\n                                    } else {\n                                        if (mode == 'insert') {\n                                            $('a.attend[val=' + event_type + ']', curActObj).addClass('clicked');\n                                        } else {\n                                            $('a.attend', curActObj).toggleClass('clicked');\n                                        }\n                                        curActObj.find('.textdetailbig').first().html(res.contents);\n
